pier	"<img src=""30_3594.jpg"" />"	[sound:30_3594.mp3]	[sound:30_3594_meaning.mp3]	[sound:30_3594_example.mp3]	A <i>pier</i> is a structure that extends into a body of water.	If you want to catch bigger fish, then go to the far end of the <b>pier</b>.	[piər]

tariff	"<img src=""30_3596.jpg"" />"	[sound:30_3596.mp3]	[sound:30_3596_meaning.mp3]	[sound:30_3596_example.mp3]	A <i>tarif</i> is a tax or fee paid on certain imports or exports.	Our <b>tarif</b> on imported wool makes foreign wool more expensive.	[tǽrif]
